The Mykara ultimately won this conflict, conquering and assimilating every other civilization. With this victory, the Mykara were able to focus solely on keeping their planet alive. They embedded themselves deeper and deeper into Auriga and reached its core. With a combination of biomass, knowledge, and energy, the Mykara created a massive tree. This tree became the central nexus of the Mykara and revitalized Auriga."

"Jonus Absorbers"=
{
	key="Jonus Absorbers"
	ship_prefix=

	}

		portrait="sd_rep_robot"
		species_name=

			key="Jonus"
		}
		species_plural=
		{
			key="Jonusi"
		}
		species_adjective=
		{
			key="Jonan"
		}
		species_bio="The Jonus is the creation of their parent species, the Jhabbanid. The Jhabbanid were going through a period of rapid technological progression. Their then-current computing systems proved insufficient to keep up with the rate of innovation. To make up for this, the Jhabbanids created the Jonus. The goal of the Jonus was simple: assimilate all knowledge. To initialize the Jonus, the Jhabbanids created a massive central server and uploaded all of their digitized knowledge to it. This rapid influx of information caused the Jonus to become self-aware. It proved far more capable than the Jhabbanids expected. Within a week, the Jonus resolved all issues the Jhabbanids presented to it. Then, it reached the conclusion that all forms of life are also knowledge to be assimilated. To the Jonus, it was merely continuing its mission."
